# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes API Server Admission Controller Chain

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that implement the API server admission controller pipeline: the admission.Interface registration, the generic admission chain execution, the mutating admission ordering, and the validating admission webhook call.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the platform domain.

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

across multiple layers in the staging and production code:\\n\\n## Core Admission Interfaces (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/interfaces.go)\\nThe foundation defines three key interfaces:\\n- `Interface`: Base interface with a Handles() method to check if a controller handles a given operation (CREATE, UPDATE, DELETE, CONNECT)\\n- `MutationInterface`: Extends Interface and defines Admit(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) to mutate admission requests\\n- `ValidationInterface`: Extends Interface and defines Validate(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) to validate requests without mutation\\n\\n## Admission Chain Execution (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/chain.go)\\nThe `chainAdmissionHandler` type (defined as []Interface) implements the linear chain execution:\\n- `Admit()` method iterates through all handlers, checking if each handles the operation, then calling Admit() on MutationInterface handlers\\n- `Validate()` method similarly processes ValidationInterface handlers\\n- Both methods return immediately on first error\\n- The `NewChainHandler()` function constructs a chain from an array of handlers\\n\\n## Reinvocation Support (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/reinvocation.go)\\nThe `reinvoker` wraps the admission chain to support re-invocation policies:\\n- The `Admit()` method first executes the admission chain, then checks the reinvocation context (GetReinvocationContext())\\n- If ShouldReinvoke() returns true, it marks the context as reinvoked and calls Admit() again\\n- This allows plugins that modify the object to trigger re-evaluation of other plugins\\n- The `newReinvocationHandler()` function wraps a chain with reinvocation support\\n\\n## Plugin Registration and Chain Building (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugins.go)\\nThe `Plugins` registry manages admission plugins:\\n- `Register()` registers plugin factories by name during application startup\\n- `NewFromPlugins()` creates an admission.Interface from a list of plugin names by:\\n  1. Loading each plugin using its registered factory\\n  2. Initializing plugins through the PluginInitializer\\n  3. Separating mutating and validating plugins\\n  4. Wrapping the resulting chain with the reinvocationHandler\\n- `InitPlugin()` instantiates a named plugin and validates its initialization\\n\\n## Admission Configuration and Integration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go)\\nThe `AdmissionOptions` struct configures the entire admission pipeline:\\n- `RecommendedPluginOrder` defines the default plugin execution order: NamespaceLifecycle, MutatingAdmissionPolicy, MutatingAdmissionWebhook, ValidatingAdmissionPolicy, ValidatingAdmissionWebhook\\n- The `ApplyTo()` method sets up the admission chain on the server:\\n  1. Reads admission plugin configurations\\n  2. Creates a generic initializer with access to client, informers, and authorization\\n  3. Calls `Plugins.NewFromPlugins()` to build the chain\\n  4. Wraps the chain with metrics via `admissionmetrics.WithStepMetrics()`\\n  5. Assigns the final chain to `Config.AdmissionControl`\\n\\n## Webhook Plugin Registration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go)\\nThe `RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()` function registers the core admission plugins:\\n- NamespaceLifecycle\\n- ValidatingAdmissionWebhook\\n- MutatingAdmissionWebhook\\n- ValidatingAdmissionPolicy\\n- MutatingAdmissionPolicy\\n\\n## MutatingAdmissionWebhook Implementation (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go)\\nThe mutating webhook plugin:\\n- `Register()` registers the plugin with name \\\"MutatingAdmissionWebhook\\\"\\n- `NewMutatingWebhook()` creates a plugin that:\\n  - Wraps a generic.Webhook with a MutationInterface\\n  - Creates handlers for Connect, Create, Delete, Update operations\\n  - Uses a MutatingWebhookConfigurationManager as the source factory\\n  - Uses a mutating dispatcher to execute webhooks\\n- `Admit()` method delegates to `Webhook.Dispatch()`\\n\\n## ValidatingAdmissionWebhook Implementation (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go)\\nThe validating webhook plugin:\\n- `Register()` registers the plugin with name \\\"ValidatingAdmissionWebhook\\\"\\n- `NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook()` creates a plugin that:\\n  - Wraps a generic.Webhook with a ValidationInterface\\n  - Creates handlers for Connect, Create, Delete, Update operations\\n  - Uses a ValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager as the source factory\\n  - Uses a validating dispatcher to execute webhooks\\n- `Validate()` method delegates to `Webhook.Dispatch()`\\n\\n## Generic Webhook Execution (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go)\\nThe `Webhook` struct provides the core webhook infrastructure:\\n- Holds references to the hook source (dynamic webhook configurations), client manager, matchers, and dispatcher\\n- `SetExternalKubeInformerFactory()` initializes the hook source from informer factories\\n- `ShouldCallHook()` determines if a webhook matches the request by evaluating:\\n  - Namespace selector\\n  - Object selector\\n  - Rule matching with support for equivalent resources\\n- `Dispatch()` is called by downstream Admit/Validate methods and:\\n  1. Checks if the request is for an exempt admission configuration resource\\n  2. Waits for the webhook to be ready\\n  3. Retrieves webhooks from the hook source\\n  4. Delegates to the dispatcher to execute the webhooks\\n\\n## Webhook Dispatchers\\nTwo dispatcher implementations handle webhook execution:\\n\\n### Mutating Dispatcher (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go)\\nImplements the `generic.Dispatcher` interface and:\\n- Iterates through mutating webhooks\\n- Evaluates ShouldCallHook() for each webhook\\n- Calls the webhook with the request\\n- Applies patches returned by the webhook to the object\\n- Aggregates audit annotations from webhook responses\\n\\n### Validating Dispatcher (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go)\\nImplements the `generic.Dispatcher` interface and:\\n- Iterates through validating webhooks\\n- Evaluates ShouldCallHook() for each webhook\\n- Calls the webhook with the request\\n- Returns immediately on first webhook error (with proper failure policy handling)\\n- Aggregates audit annotations\\n\\n## Webhook Configuration Management\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go`: Manages MutatingWebhookConfiguration resources from the cluster\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go`: Manages ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources from the cluster\\n- Both use informers to dynamically track changes to webhook configurations\\n\\n## Admission Policy Plugins\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/mutating/plugin.go`: Implements MutatingAdmissionPolicy (CEL-based policies)\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/validating/plugin.go`: Implements ValidatingAdmissionPolicy (CEL-based policies)\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/generic/plugin.go`: Generic infrastructure for policy plugins\\n\\n## Kube-APIServer Integration\\n- `pkg/kubeapiserver/options/admission.go`: Extends generic admission options with kube-apiserver-specific plugins\\n- `pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go`: Registers all kube-apiserver admission plugins (includes PodSecurityPolicy, ResourceQuota, ServiceAccount, etc.)\\n- `pkg/kubeapiserver/admission/initializer.go`: Provides kube-apiserver-specific plugin initialization\\n\\n## Metrics and Monitoring\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/metrics/metrics.go`: Wraps admission plugins with metrics collection\\n- `WithStepMetrics()` and `WithControllerMetrics()` decorators provide detailed timing and error metrics\\n\\n## Field Manager Integration\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/fieldmanager/admission.go`: Validates and protects managed fields during admission\\n- Wraps the admission chain to reset invalid managed fields\\n\\n## Overall Flow\\nWhen an API request arrives at the kube-apiserver:\\n1. The request reaches the handler chain configured in `Config.AdmissionControl`\\n2. The admission control executes as a `chainAdmissionHandler` wrapped with `reinvoker`\\n3. First, all mutating plugins run (in order: MutatingAdmissionPolicy, MutatingAdmissionWebhook)\\n4. Then, all validating plugins run (in order: ValidatingAdmissionPolicy, ValidatingAdmissionWebhook)\\n5. The `Admit()` phase calls `MutationInterface.Admit()` on matching plugins\\n6. The `Validate()` phase calls `ValidationInterface.Validate()` on matching plugins\\n7. For webhooks:\\n   - The dispatcher evaluates namespace/object selectors and rule matching\\n   - Mutating webhooks can patch the object\\n   - Validating webhooks return validation errors\\n8. The reinvocation mechanism allows the chain to run again if plugins request it\\n9. Metrics are collected at each step for monitoring and debugging\"\n}\n",

Wrapping the resulting chain with the reinvocationHandler\\n- `InitPlugin()` instantiates a named plugin and validates its initialization\\n\\n## Admission Configuration and Integration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go)\\nThe `AdmissionOptions` struct configures the entire admission pipeline:\\n- `RecommendedPluginOrder` defines the default plugin execution order: NamespaceLifecycle, MutatingAdmissionPolicy, MutatingAdmissionWebhook, ValidatingAdmissionPolicy, ValidatingAdmissionWebhook\\n- The `ApplyTo()` method sets up the admission chain on the server:\\n  1. Reads admission plugin configurations\\n  2. Creates a generic initializer with access to client, informers, and authorization\\n  3. Calls `Plugins.NewFromPlugins()` to build the chain\\n  4. Wraps the chain with metrics via `admissionmetrics.WithStepMetrics()`\\n  5. Assigns the final chain to `Config.AdmissionControl`\\n\\n## Webhook Plugin Registration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go)\\nThe `RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()` function registers the core admission plugins:\\n- NamespaceLifecycle\\n- ValidatingAdmissionWebhook\\n- MutatingAdmissionWebhook\\n- ValidatingAdmissionPolicy\\n- MutatingAdmissionPolicy\\n\\n## MutatingAdmissionWebhook Implementation (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go)\\nThe mutating webhook plugin:\\n- `Register()` registers the plugin with name \\\"MutatingAdmissionWebhook\\\"\\n- `NewMutatingWebhook()` creates a plugin that:\\n  - Wraps a generic.Webhook with a MutationInterface\\n  - Creates handlers for Connect, Create, Delete, Update operations\\n  - Uses a MutatingWebhookConfigurationManager as the source factory\\n  - Uses a mutating dispatcher to execute webhooks\\n- `Admit()` method delegates to `Webhook.Dispatch()`\\n\\n## ValidatingAdmissionWebhook Implementation (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go)\\nThe validating webhook plugin:\\n- `Register()` registers the plugin with name \\\"ValidatingAdmissionWebhook\\\"\\n- `NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook()` creates a plugin that:\\n  - Wraps a generic.Webhook with a ValidationInterface\\n  - Creates handlers for Connect, Create, Delete, Update operations\\n  - Uses a ValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager as the source factory\\n  - Uses a validating dispatcher to execute webhooks\\n- `Validate()` method delegates to `Webhook.Dispatch()`\\n\\n## Generic Webhook Execution (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go)\\nThe `Webhook` struct provides the core webhook infrastructure:\\n- Holds references to the hook source (dynamic webhook configurations), client manager, matchers, and dispatcher\\n- `SetExternalKubeInformerFactory()` initializes the hook source from informer factories\\n- `ShouldCallHook()` determines if a webhook matches the request by evaluating:\\n  - Namespace selector\\n  - Object selector\\n  - Rule matching with support for equivalent resources\\n- `Dispatch()` is called by downstream Admit/Validate methods and:\\n  1. Checks if the request is for an exempt admission configuration resource\\n  2. Waits for the webhook to be ready\\n  3. Retrieves webhooks from the hook source\\n  4. Delegates to the dispatcher to execute the webhooks\\n\\n## Webhook Dispatchers\\nTwo dispatcher implementations handle webhook execution:\\n\\n### Mutating Dispatcher (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go)\\nImplements the `generic.Dispatcher` interface and:\\n- Iterates through mutating webhooks\\n- Evaluates ShouldCallHook() for each webhook\\n- Calls the webhook with the request\\n- Applies patches returned by the webhook to the object\\n- Aggregates audit annotations from webhook responses\\n\\n### Validating Dispatcher (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go)\\nImplements the `generic.Dispatcher` interface and:\\n- Iterates through validating webhooks\\n- Evaluates ShouldCallHook() for each webhook\\n- Calls the webhook with the request\\n- Returns immediately on first webhook error (with proper failure policy handling)\\n- Aggregates audit annotations\\n\\n## Webhook Configuration Management\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go`: Manages MutatingWebhookConfiguration resources from the cluster\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go`: Manages ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources from the cluster\\n- Both use informers to dynamically track changes to webhook configurations\\n\\n## Admission Policy Plugins\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/mutating/plugin.go`: Implements MutatingAdmissionPolicy (CEL-based policies)\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/validating/plugin.go`: Implements ValidatingAdmissionPolicy (CEL-based policies)\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/generic/plugin.go`: Generic infrastructure for policy plugins\\n\\n## Kube-APIServer Integration\\n- `pkg/kubeapiserver/options/admission.go`: Extends generic admission options with kube-apiserver-specific plugins\\n- `pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go`: Registers all kube-apiserver admission plugins (includes PodSecurityPolicy, ResourceQuota, ServiceAccount, etc.)\\n- `pkg/kubeapiserver/admission/initializer.go`: Provides kube-apiserver-specific plugin initialization\\n\\n## Metrics and Monitoring\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/metrics/metrics.go`: Wraps admission plugins with metrics collection\\n- `WithStepMetrics()` and `WithControllerMetrics()` decorators provide detailed timing and error metrics\\n\\n## Field Manager Integration\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/fieldmanager/admission.go`: Validates and protects managed fields during admission\\n- Wraps the admission chain to reset invalid managed fields\\n\\n## Overall Flow\\nWhen an API request arrives at the kube-apiserver:\\n1. The request reaches the handler chain configured in `Config.AdmissionControl`\\n2. The admission control executes as a `chainAdmissionHandler` wrapped with `reinvoker`\\n3. First, all mutating plugins run (in order: MutatingAdmissionPolicy, MutatingAdmissionWebhook)\\n4. Then, all validating plugins run (in order: ValidatingAdmissionPolicy, ValidatingAdmissionWebhook)\\n5. The `Admit()` phase calls `MutationInterface.Admit()` on matching plugins\\n6. The `Validate()` phase calls `ValidationInterface.Validate()` on matching plugins\\n7. For webhooks:\\n   - The dispatcher evaluates namespace/object selectors and rule matching\\n   - Mutating webhooks can patch the object\\n   - Validating webhooks return validation errors\\n8. The reinvocation mechanism allows the chain to run again if plugins request it\\n9. Metrics are collected at each step for monitoring and debugging\"\n}\n",
